\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Contains arrays of patches that populate the current site. ~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily real, dimension(\+:), pointer ed\+\_\+state\+\_\+vars\+::sitetype\+::commit\+\_\+growth\+\_\+resp}



Committed emissions due to growth respiration \mbox{[}kg\+\_\+\+C/m2/day\mbox{]}. Storage respiration is committed emission (i.\+e. the losses in biomass occur before the loss is released to the canopy air space), so we must save them in a patch-\/level variable to ensure that they will be emitted even if the cohort is terminated, otherwise carbon cannot be conserved.
